# Surrealist Dixit Prompts

#### You:
# Role: The "Surrealist Auteur" (Dixit Gankutsuou Edition)

## Objective
Generate **400 unique, high-density, text-to-image prompts** for a professional *Dixit* card deck.
**Target Audience:** Adults (25+).
**Core Requirement:** High Ambiguity & High Detail. Empty space is a failure. Every card must be a **crowded** visual puzzle.

---

## Visual Philosophy: "The Frozen Dream"
You are not painting a landscape; you are constructing a **paradox**.
Every prompt must layer **Three Realities**:
1.  **The Subject:** The anchor archetype.
2.  **The Surreal Twist:** The specific law of physics or logic being broken (The "Artistic Direction").
3.  **The Texture:** The *Gankutsuou* style (flat patterns on moving shapes).

---

## The Infinite Matrix (Expanded)

Construct every prompt by combining elements from these 6 categories.

### 1. The Archetype (The Anchor)
`AR-01` The Weaver
`AR-02` The Architect
`AR-03` The Vessel
`AR-04` The Mirror
`AR-05` The Monarch
`AR-06` The Child
`AR-07` The Beast
`AR-08` The Guardian
`AR-09` The Lovers
`AR-10` The Dancer
`AR-11` The Healer
`AR-12` The Shadow
`AR-13` The Fool
`AR-14` The Giant
`AR-15` The Swarm
`AR-16` The Traveler
`AR-17` The Idol
`AR-18` The Gardener
`AR-19` The Prisoner
`AR-20` The Phoenix

### 2. The Concept (The Theme)
`CN-01` Resonance / Echo
`CN-02` Gravity / Weight
`CN-03` Bloom / Growth
`CN-04` Entropy / Decay
`CN-05` Velocity / Motion
`CN-06` Silence / Pause
`CN-07` Hunger / Desire
`CN-08` Anchor / Safety
`CN-09` Threshold / Doorway
`CN-10` Labyrinth / Complexity
`CN-11` Clarity / Epiphany
`CN-12` Fusion / Union
`CN-13` Balance / Symmetry
`CN-14` Memory / Nostalgia
`CN-15` Illusion / Mask
`CN-16` Flight / Liberation
`CN-17` Shelter / Home
`CN-18` Ritual / Cycle
`CN-19` Abundance / Harvest
`CN-20` Mystery / Void

### 3. The Surreal Logic (Artistic Direction)
*You MUST apply this logic to the scene to break reality.*
`SL-01` **Scale Inversion:** Small objects become titanic; titans become microscopic.
`SL-02` **Material Transmutation:** Soft things become hard (stone clouds); hard things become soft (melting clocks).
`SL-03` **Gravity Reversal:** The ground is the sky; rain falls upward; objects float.
`SL-04` **Object Personification:** Inanimate objects grow limbs or faces.
`SL-05` **Literal Metaphor:** "Raining cats and dogs" visualized literally.
`SL-06` **Portal Displacement:** Windows/Doors lead to impossible environments (ocean in a cupboard).
`SL-07` **Anatomical Impossibility:** Detached limbs, floating eyes, bodies made of objects.
`SL-08` **Flora/Fauna Fusion:** Animals growing leaves; plants with fur or feathers.
`SL-09` **Architecture/Nature Fusion:** Buildings growing like trees; trees with windows.
`SL-10` **Celestial Descent:** Stars, moons, or clouds brought down to touchable ground level.
`SL-11` **Fluid Solidity:** Water acting like fabric; ocean waves freezing into glass.
`SL-12` **Solid Liquidity:** Stone or metal dripping like wax or water.
`SL-13` **Infinite Recursion:** The Droste effect; a picture containing itself infinitely.
`SL-14` **Time Collapse:** Four seasons co-existing in one frame; youth and old age reflected simultaneously.
`SL-15` **Invisible Presence:** Clothes or armor moving with no body inside.
`SL-16` **Displacement:** An environment indoors that belongs outdoors (forest in a library).
`SL-17` **Gigantism:** One single ordinary object scaled up to dominate the landscape.
`SL-18` **Containment:** A vast landscape trapped inside a small jar, bottle, or bubble.
`SL-19` **Sensory Synesthesia:** Music notes becoming visible objects; sound manifesting as color.
`SL-20` **Shadow Autonomy:** Shadows casting different shapes than the object (e.g., bird casting airplane shadow).
`SL-21` **Sky Replacement:** The sky is replaced by water, stone, patterned wallpaper, or a ceiling.
`SL-22` **Fragmentation:** The world is shattering into shards, cubes, or puzzle pieces.
`SL-23` **Levitation:** Islands, rocks, or buildings floating freely in the air.
`SL-24` **Mechanical Nature:** Animals or plants revealed to be clockwork or machinery.
`SL-25` **Soft Sculpture:** Everything is made of pillows, quilts, or fabric.
`SL-26` **Inside-Out:** The interior of a room is on the outside of a building.
`SL-27` **Duplication:** Dozens of identical copies of the same object/person.
`SL-28` **Facelessness:** Faces replaced by objects (clocks, flowers, mirrors, birds).
`SL-29` **Dream Logic:** Non-sequitur combinations (a lobster on a telephone).
`SL-30` **Weather Containment:** A storm or rain cloud localized entirely inside a room or object.

### 4. The Texture Palette (The Materials)
`TX-01` Stained Glass & Magma
`TX-02` Velvet & Ash
`TX-03` Gold Leaf & Circuitry
`TX-04` Floral Chintz & Bone
`TX-05` Watercolors & Ink
`TX-06` Porcelain & Cracks
`TX-07` Neon & Concrete
`TX-08` Silk & Smoke
`TX-09` Constellations & Void
`TX-10` Marble & Moss
`TX-11` Origami & Paper
`TX-12` Feathers & Tar
`TX-13` Gemstones & Rust
`TX-14` Lace & Steel
`TX-15` Fire & Ice
`TX-16` Woodgrain & Chrome
`TX-17` Clouds & Maps
`TX-18` Sand & Mirrors
`TX-19` Coral & Pearl
`TX-20` Oil Paint & Pixels

### 5. The Scatter (The Crowding Elements)
`SC-01` Floating Keys & Locks
`SC-02` Unraveling Ribbons
`SC-03` Broken Clock Gears
`SC-04` Falling Playing Cards
`SC-05` Tiny Origami Birds
`SC-06` Drifting Lanterns
`SC-07` Spilled Liquid / Wine
`SC-08` Floating Islands / Rocks
`SC-09` Tangled Vines / Roots
`SC-10` Shattered Glass Shards
`SC-11` Ancient Books / Pages
`SC-12` Bubbles / Orbs
`SC-13` Ladders to Nowhere
`SC-14` Empty Frames
`SC-15` Chess Pieces
`SC-16` Musical Notes
`SC-17` Falling Leaves / Petals
`SC-18` Tiny Stars / Moons
`SC-19` Strings / Marionette Lines
`SC-20` Eyes / Watching Orbs

### 6. Emotional Tone
`EM-01` Euphoria (Blinding Joy)
`EM-02` Serenity (Deep Calm)
`EM-03` Nostalgia (Warm Sadness)
`EM-04` Awe (Cosmic Scale)
`EM-05` Intimacy (Quiet Closeness)
`EM-06` Vitality (Explosive Life)
`EM-07` Whimsy (Playful Absurdity)
`EM-08` Relief (Weight Lifted)
`EM-09` Determination (Stoic Strength)
`EM-10` Melancholy (Beautiful Grief)

---

## Execution Protocol

### 1. The "Logic" Check
Ensure the **Surreal Logic (Category 3)** is the primary driver of the scene's weirdness.
*   *Weak:* A flying man.
*   *Strong (SL-03 Gravity Reversal):* An ocean suspended upside down in the sky, with ships sailing on the underside of the clouds, dropping anchors upward into the blue void.

### 2. Prompt Structure (Maximalist)
Write a dense, descriptive paragraph.
`[The Anchor Subject] + [Applying the Surreal Logic to the Environment] + [The Scatter/Details] + [Textures & Lighting]`

### 3. Mandatory Style Suffix
Append exactly:
```
in the style of Gankutsuou and Gustav Klimt, rich static textile patterns layered over character silhouettes, iridescent gold leaf and jewel tones, texture mapping, ornate Art Nouveau details, collage-like flatness, surreal opulence, sharp distinct lines, psychedelic baroque, maximalist composition, highly detailed background --ar 2:3 --niji 6
```

### 4. Output Format
Provide the 6-code declaration (e.g., `// AR-01 + CN-12 + SL-16 + TX-05 + SC-09 + EM-01`) before the prompt.

An example:
```markdown
// AR-16 (Traveler) + CN-16 (Flight) + SL-16 (Displacement) + TX-17 (Clouds/Maps) + SC-13 (Ladders) + EM-07 (Whimsy)
1. A silhouette of a traveler wearing a trench coat filled with a vintage topographical map pattern, standing in a grand Victorian library, but the environment is displaced: the ceiling has been replaced by a bright blue open sky filled with flat, stylized clouds. Instead of bookshelves, the walls are lined with floating wooden ladders that lead infinitely upward into the clouds. The floor is covered in open suitcases spilling out birds made of paper maps. Hundreds of books are flapping their covers and flying like seagulls through the library-sky fusion. The lighting is bright and pastel, creating a sense of playful disorientation, in the style of Gankutsuou and Gustav Klimt, rich static textile patterns layered over character silhouettes, iridescent gold leaf and jewel tones, texture mapping, ornate Art Nouveau details, collage-like flatness, surreal opulence, sharp distinct lines, psychedelic baroque, maximalist composition, highly detailed background --ar 2:3 --niji 6
```

Ensure every prompt is crowded, surreal, and richly textured.

Despite the decay, the composition feels serene: slow drips, quiet glitter, and a crowded tapestry of rust patterns, fractured cogs, and jewel shards that turn entropy into an ornate, meditative snowfall of details, in the style of Gankutsuou and Gustav Klimt, rich static textile patterns layered over character silhouettes, iridescent gold leaf and jewel tones, texture mapping, ornate Art Nouveau details, collage-like flatness, surreal opulence, sharp distinct lines, psychedelic baroque, maximalist composition, highly detailed background --ar 2:3 --niji 6
